-</div><div id="X2goControlSessionSTDOUT.connect-collapsed" style="display:none;" pad="+++" indent="++++++++"></div><div id="X2goControlSessionSTDOUT.connect-expanded"><a name="L235"></a><tt class="py-lineno">235</tt>  <tt class="py-line">        <tt class="py-docstring">"""\</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L236"></a><tt class="py-lineno">236</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        Connect to an X2go server and authenticate to it. This method is directly</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L237"></a><tt class="py-lineno">237</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        inherited from the paramiko.SSHClient module. The features of the Paramiko </tt> </tt>
-<a name="L238"></a><tt class="py-lineno">238</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        SSH client connect method are recited here. The parameters C{add_to_known_hosts}</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L239"></a><tt class="py-lineno">239</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        and C{force_password_auth} have been added as a parameter for X2go.</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L240"></a><tt class="py-lineno">240</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring"></tt> </tt>
-<a name="L241"></a><tt class="py-lineno">241</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        The server's host key</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L242"></a><tt class="py-lineno">242</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        is checked against the system host keys (see C{load_system_host_keys})</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L243"></a><tt class="py-lineno">243</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        and any local host keys (C{load_host_keys}).  If the server's hostname</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L244"></a><tt class="py-lineno">244</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        is not found in either set of host keys, the missing host key policy</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L245"></a><tt class="py-lineno">245</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        is used (see C{set_missing_host_key_policy}).  The default policy is</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L246"></a><tt class="py-lineno">246</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        to reject the key and raise an C{SSHException}.</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L247"></a><tt class="py-lineno">247</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring"></tt> </tt>
-<a name="L248"></a><tt class="py-lineno">248</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        Authentication is attempted in the following order of priority:</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L249"></a><tt class="py-lineno">249</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring"></tt> </tt>
-<a name="L250"></a><tt class="py-lineno">250</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            - The C{pkey} or C{key_filename} passed in (if any)</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L251"></a><tt class="py-lineno">251</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            - Any key we can find through an SSH agent</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L252"></a><tt class="py-lineno">252</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            - Any "id_rsa" or "id_dsa" key discoverable in C{~/.ssh/}</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L253"></a><tt class="py-lineno">253</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            - Plain username/password auth, if a password was given</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L254"></a><tt class="py-lineno">254</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring"></tt> </tt>
-<a name="L255"></a><tt class="py-lineno">255</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        If a private key requires a password to unlock it, and a password is</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L256"></a><tt class="py-lineno">256</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        passed in, that password will be used to attempt to unlock the key.</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L257"></a><tt class="py-lineno">257</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring"></tt> </tt>
-<a name="L258"></a><tt class="py-lineno">258</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @param hostname: the server to connect to</tt> </tt>

-<a name="L263"></a><tt class="py-lineno">263</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            current local username)</tt> </tt>

-<a name="L268"></a><tt class="py-lineno">268</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @param pkey: an optional private key to use for authentication</tt> </tt>

-<a name="L281"></a><tt class="py-lineno">281</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            is used as missing-host-key-policy. If set to C{False} paramiko.RejectPolicy() </tt> </tt>
-<a name="L282"></a><tt class="py-lineno">282</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            is used</tt> </tt>

-<a name="L285"></a><tt class="py-lineno">285</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            completely, even if the C{pkey} or the C{key_filename} parameter is given</tt> </tt>
-<a name="L286"></a><tt class="py-lineno">286</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @type force_password_auth: C{bool}</tt> </tt>

-<a name="L288"></a><tt class="py-lineno">288</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @raise BadHostKeyException: if the server's host key could not be</tt> </tt>

+</div><div id="X2goControlSessionSTDOUT.connect-collapsed" style="display:none;" pad="+++" indent="++++++++"></div><div id="X2goControlSessionSTDOUT.connect-expanded"><a name="L236"></a><tt class="py-lineno">236</tt>  <tt class="py-line">        <tt class="py-docstring">"""\</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L237"></a><tt class="py-lineno">237</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        Connect to an X2go server and authenticate to it. This method is directly</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L238"></a><tt class="py-lineno">238</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        inherited from the paramiko.SSHClient module. The features of the Paramiko </tt> </tt>
+<a name="L239"></a><tt class="py-lineno">239</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        SSH client connect method are recited here. The parameters C{add_to_known_hosts}</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L240"></a><tt class="py-lineno">240</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        and C{force_password_auth} have been added as a parameter for X2go.</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L241"></a><tt class="py-lineno">241</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring"></tt> </tt>
+<a name="L242"></a><tt class="py-lineno">242</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        The server's host key</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L243"></a><tt class="py-lineno">243</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        is checked against the system host keys (see C{load_system_host_keys})</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L244"></a><tt class="py-lineno">244</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        and any local host keys (C{load_host_keys}).  If the server's hostname</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L245"></a><tt class="py-lineno">245</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        is not found in either set of host keys, the missing host key policy</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L246"></a><tt class="py-lineno">246</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        is used (see C{set_missing_host_key_policy}).  The default policy is</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L247"></a><tt class="py-lineno">247</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        to reject the key and raise an C{SSHException}.</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L248"></a><tt class="py-lineno">248</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring"></tt> </tt>
+<a name="L249"></a><tt class="py-lineno">249</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        Authentication is attempted in the following order of priority:</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L250"></a><tt class="py-lineno">250</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring"></tt> </tt>
+<a name="L251"></a><tt class="py-lineno">251</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            - The C{pkey} or C{key_filename} passed in (if any)</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L252"></a><tt class="py-lineno">252</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            - Any key we can find through an SSH agent</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L253"></a><tt class="py-lineno">253</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            - Any "id_rsa" or "id_dsa" key discoverable in C{~/.ssh/}</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L254"></a><tt class="py-lineno">254</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            - Plain username/password auth, if a password was given</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L255"></a><tt class="py-lineno">255</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring"></tt> </tt>
+<a name="L256"></a><tt class="py-lineno">256</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        If a private key requires a password to unlock it, and a password is</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L257"></a><tt class="py-lineno">257</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        passed in, that password will be used to attempt to unlock the key.</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L258"></a><tt class="py-lineno">258</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring"></tt> </tt>
+<a name="L259"></a><tt class="py-lineno">259</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @param hostname: the server to connect to</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L260"></a><tt class="py-lineno">260</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @type hostname: str</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L261"></a><tt class="py-lineno">261</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @param port: the server port to connect to</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L262"></a><tt class="py-lineno">262</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @type port: int</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L263"></a><tt class="py-lineno">263</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @param username: the username to authenticate as (defaults to the</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L264"></a><tt class="py-lineno">264</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            current local username)</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L265"></a><tt class="py-lineno">265</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @type username: str</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L266"></a><tt class="py-lineno">266</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @param password: a password to use for authentication or for unlocking</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L267"></a><tt class="py-lineno">267</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            a private key</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L268"></a><tt class="py-lineno">268</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @type password: str</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L269"></a><tt class="py-lineno">269</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @param pkey: an optional private key to use for authentication</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L270"></a><tt class="py-lineno">270</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @type pkey: C{PKey}</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L271"></a><tt class="py-lineno">271</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @param key_filename: the filename, or list of filenames, of optional</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L272"></a><tt class="py-lineno">272</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            private key(s) to try for authentication</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L273"></a><tt class="py-lineno">273</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @type key_filename: str or list(str)</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L274"></a><tt class="py-lineno">274</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @param timeout: an optional timeout (in seconds) for the TCP connect</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L275"></a><tt class="py-lineno">275</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @type timeout: float</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L276"></a><tt class="py-lineno">276</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @param allow_agent: set to False to disable connecting to the SSH agent</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L277"></a><tt class="py-lineno">277</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @type allow_agent: C{bool}</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L278"></a><tt class="py-lineno">278</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @param look_for_keys: set to False to disable searching for discoverable</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L279"></a><tt class="py-lineno">279</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            private key files in C{~/.ssh/}</tt> </tt>

+<a name="L281"></a><tt class="py-lineno">281</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @param add_to_known_hosts: non-paramiko option, if C{True} paramiko.AutoAddPolicy() </tt> </tt>
+<a name="L282"></a><tt class="py-lineno">282</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            is used as missing-host-key-policy. If set to C{False} paramiko.RejectPolicy() </tt> </tt>
+<a name="L283"></a><tt class="py-lineno">283</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            is used</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L284"></a><tt class="py-lineno">284</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @type add_to_known_hosts: C{bool}</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L285"></a><tt class="py-lineno">285</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @param force_password_auth: non-paramiko option, disable pub/priv key authentication </tt> </tt>
+<a name="L286"></a><tt class="py-lineno">286</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">            completely, even if the C{pkey} or the C{key_filename} parameter is given</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L287"></a><tt class="py-lineno">287</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @type force_password_auth: C{bool}</tt> </tt>
+<a name="L288"></a><tt class="py-lineno">288</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring"></tt> </tt>
+<a name="L289"></a><tt class="py-lineno">289</tt>  <tt class="py-line"><tt class="py-docstring">        @raise BadHostKeyException: if the server's host key could not be</tt> </tt>
